Contact Us
#  Let the experts help you **get stuff done.**
![A group photo of the DCED BusinessPA team, alongside Governor Josh Shapiro, smiling at the camera during the BusinessPA Launch Reception at the Governor's Residence](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/governor-josh-shapiro-attends-the-businesspa-launch-reception-at-the-governors-residence_54138377470_o?fmt=webp)
## Connect with the
## **BusinessPA team**
The BusinessPA team is equipped with local experts who are eager to help your business achieve its objectives, right here in the Commonwealth. Whether you're looking to discover the benefits of doing business in PA, are exploring an expansion or relocation project, or are looking to boost your business with international trade, we're here to assist. Our white-glove approach to serving our business community means that we'll take the time to understand your organization's needs before providing a tailored solution. Plus, our vast network of resources and regional partnerships makes us the best place to start—no matter your project scope or timeline.
There's a reason we say "Pennsylvania Gets It Done" so often — it's not just a slogan, it's a promise. If you're ready to get it done for your organization, drop us a line and let us know how we can help. Already know who you're looking to contact? [Get started here.](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/about_business-pa)
* * *
## Get In Touch
## **Let us know how we can help!**

KEY INDUSTRIES
# Energy
![Sunoco Marcus Hook Natural Gas](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/sunoco_marcushook_naturalgas1?fmt=webp)
## Partner with an **Energy Powerhouse**
As the nation’s second-largest energy supplier, Pennsylvania isn't just a place — it's a powerhouse. Companies here count on low-cost, reliable access to electricity and natural gas within a future-focused energy ecosystem that’s surging with opportunity.
PA’s electric grid powers homes and businesses through diverse resources, from natural gas and nuclear power to wind and hydropower. We’re the country’s largest natural gas producer after Texas, prepared to fuel energy-intensive industries like heavy manufacturing and data processing. And we are invested in maintaining a strong grid. That’s why the Pennsylvania Department of Environmental Protection awarded over $15 million in [grants to electric distribution companies(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/agencies/dep/newsroom/shapiro-administration-awards-over-15-million-to-strengthen-rural-electric-grid-and-prevent-and-shorten-power-outages-for-nearly-60000-pennsylvanians.html#:~:text=Harrisburg%2C%20PA%20%E2%80%93%20The%20Pennsylvania%20Department,Grants%20\(PA%20GRG\)%20funding.) to enhance grid reliability and resilience.
We’ve been at the forefront of energy production for centuries, from our historic coal mines to breakthroughs in oil and nuclear power. Today, we're leading the charge in clean hydrogen technology as the [only state with two federally designated(opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/newsroom/governor-shapiro-pennsylvania-designated-as-a-regional-tech-hub-receives-strategy-development-grant/) Regional Clean Energy Hubs. Our abundant supply and steadfast commitment to innovation make Pennsylvania an ideal partner for businesses seeking reliable, sustainable, and competitive energy solutions. 
* * *
> “We’re bullish about the region’s leadership in energy innovation and transition because we have a complete and dynamic ecosystem to support it — one grounded in innovation, brain and muscle power, STEM expertise, and world-class manufacturing capacity.”
— _Stefani Pashman, CEO, Allegheny Conference on Community Development_
![Adam Walters - Senior Energy Advisor](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adam_walters_cropped)
### Adam Walters
Senior Energy Advisor
717.525.2720 | adwalters@pa.gov
CONNECT (opens in a new tab)
## In the News: PA Energy
![The founders of Verne pose for a photo in front of a blue semitruck, adorned with the company's logo, in a warehouse.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/verne-0312)
## **Verne is solving hydrogen’s hardest problem — and unlocking new power solutions**
Energy technology company Verne is tackling a longstanding challenge in clean energy: how to store hydrogen efficiently to help power industries that can’t rely on the grid. As the company looked for a world-class manufacturing ecosystem where they could expand their operation, BusinessPA’s quick, coordinated support helped Verne locate a site in Lycoming County, enabling the company to scale up quickly.
[ READ THE CASE STUDY](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/energy/case-study-verne)
![The founders of Verne pose for a photo in front of a blue semitruck, adorned with the company's logo, in a warehouse.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/verne-0312)
![PA Governor Josh Shapiro spreads wax on a made in PA snowboard. ](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/24639_gov_gilsonsnow_03)
## Commonwealth invests $4.6 million to help PMF Industries expand into the clean hydrogen market
For over 60 years, Lycoming County-based [PMF Industries, Inc(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pmfind.com/ "Link to PMF Industries website"). has manufactured precision metal components that are used in everything from aerospace to medical tech. Thanks to a new $4.6 million investment from the Commonwealth, they’re expanding into the clean hydrogen sector – creating at least 20 new full-time jobs while retaining 78 existing positions. 
[ READ THE ANNOUNCEMENT](https://pagetsitdone.com/news/creating-jobs-in-lycoming-county-shapiro-administration-investing-4-6-million-to-help-pmf-industries-expand-into-the-clean-hydrogen-market-grow-pennsylvanias-clean-energy-industry)
##  2nd Largest Net Supplier of Energy in the U.S. 
[ U.S. Energy Information Administration  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.eia.gov/state/print.php?sid=PA)
2nd Nuclear Power Producer in Nation [ U.S. Energy Information Administration  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.eia.gov/state/print.php?sid=PA)
2nd Largest Producer of Natural Gas [ U.S. Energy Information Administration  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.eia.gov/state/print.php?sid=PA)
49  Underground Gas Storage Sites [ U.S. Energy Information Administration  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.eia.gov/state/print.php?sid=PA)
3rd  Largest Coal-Producing State  [ U.S. Energy Information Administration  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.eia.gov/state/print.php?sid=PA)

## Funding & Resources
### See some of of the many programs and resources available to energy businesses in Pennsylvania.
###  Alternative and Clean Energy Program (ACE)
ACE provides financial assistance to eligible applicants for utilization, development, and construction of alternative and clean energy products, infrastructure associated with natural gas, and energy efficiency and conservation projects.
[ Learn More (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/alternative-clean-energy-program-ace/)
###  PA Department of Environmental Protection (DEP)
DEP has grants and loans to assist individuals and businesses with a host of environmental issues. Whether your project is local to your community or a statewide endeavor, DEP has tools and funding to guide you along the process.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.dep.pa.gov/Business/Pages/default.aspx)
###  Pipeline Investment Program (PIPE)
The Pipeline Investment Program (PIPE) provides grants to construct the last few miles of natural gas distribution lines to business parks, manufacturing enterprises, and industrial complexes. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/pipeline-investment-program/#.WJn9KVUrJhE)
###  Pennsylvania Energy Development Authority (PEDA)
The Pennsylvania Energy Development Authority is an independent public financing authority that funds clean, advanced energy projects. Projects that potentially qualify for funding include solar energy, wind, low-impact hydropower, geothermal, biomass, landfill gas, fuel cells, integrated gasification combined cycle, waste coal coal-mine methane, and demand management measures. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.dep.pa.gov/Business/Energy/OfficeofPollutionPrevention/FinancialOptions/Pages/PEDA.aspx)
###  Local Resource Manufacturing Tax Credit Program
The PA EDGE program provides tax credits to expanding businesses in critical manufacturing sectors. Companies purchasing dry natural gas for manufacturing petrochemicals or fertilizers may qualify for the Local Resource Manufacturing (LRM) tax credit available through the PA Department of Revenue.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.revenue.pa.gov/IncentivesCreditsPrograms/PAEDGE/Pages/Local%20Resource%20Manufacturing%20Tax%20Credit.aspx)
###  Regional Clean Hydrogen Hubs Tax Credit Program
The PA EDGE program provides tax credits to expanding businesses in critical manufacturing sectors. Manufacturers purchasing clean hydrogen and natural gas from a Regional Clean Hydrogen Hub (RCHH) many qualify for tax credits through the PA Department of Revenue.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.revenue.pa.gov/IncentivesCreditsPrograms/PAEDGE/Pages/Regional-Clean-Hydrogen-Hubs-Tax-Credit.aspx)

KEY INDUSTRIES
#  The **Most Diverse Economy** in the U.S.
![Sparks fly from a robotic arm welding sheet metal in a dark room](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/732a8957-049?fmt=webp)
## Helping Growing Industries Reach Their **Max Potential**
We're driving growth in Pennsylvania, and we're doing it with focus. Taking a data-based approach to our efforts, we have identified five key industry sectors where we should target resources and maximize opportunities for growth: **Agriculture** , **Energy** , **Life Sciences** , **Manufacturing** , and **Robotics and Technology**. The Shapiro Administration's ambitious [Ten-Year Strategic Plan for Economic Development in Pennsylvania(opens in a new tab)](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/documents/economicdevelopmentstrategy-dced_2024_final.pdf) - the first one created for Pennsylvania in nearly twenty years - sets forth a plan to bolster economic development in these industries through smart investments and public-private partnerships. Focusing on these sectors will enable us to build out industry clusters in high-growth, high-value industry segments, and to double down in industries of historic and economic significance to PA. 
Life Sciences and Robotics and Technology are high-growth areas where we can harness existing assets and accelerate the growth of our economy through selective and targeted investments. Manufacturing, Agriculture, and Energy are areas where we can leverage historic economic strengths, existing skills, and expertise to protect our built-in advantage. The quality of these jobs matters, and by focusing on these industries we will position Pennsylvania to compete for high-wage, family-sustaining jobs in all regions of the Commonwealth.
### [Agriculture ](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/agriculture)
### [Energy ](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/energy)
### [Life Sciences ](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/life_sciences)
### [Manufacturing ](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/manufacturing)
### [Robotics & Technology ](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/robotics_and_technology)
![](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-pagid/newsletterpalogo.svg)

Key Industries
# Agriculture 
![Aerial view of an indoor farm, with plants viewable through the transparent roof](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/23180_gov_littleleaf_dz_005?fmt=webp)
## Cultivating the **Future of Agriculture**
Pennsylvania agriculture feeds the nation and fuels our state’s economy. Bringing in over $132 billion annually and supporting more than 593,000 jobs, our agriculture industry is one of the most robust in the country. And it’s no wonder why: PA provides optimal conditions for farms and agribusinesses to thrive with a temperate climate, fertile soils, and convenient access to a large portion of the population.
We lead the nation in a diverse range of agricultural commodities — from dairy, livestock, and poultry to specialty crops like mushrooms, apples, peaches, and beer. You’ll also find us among the top three states for overall organic sales. By investing in innovation and embracing AgTech in the field, the Commonwealth is committed to farming sustainably and revolutionizing the way we grow food.
We take snacks and sweets seriously too, and not just in York County, the “Snack Food Capital of the World.” Pennsylvania ranks in the top five for snack food manufacturing and is home to well-known brands such as Hershey, Utz, Herr’s, and Snyder’s of Hanover. With strong agricultural resources across the state and [close proximity to major U.S. markets](https://pagetsitdone.com/why-pa/location_and_infrastructure), it’s easy for businesses here to deliver their products from farm to table.
Plant your roots in Pennsylvania and cultivate the future. 
* * *
> We're very excited about the agriculture innovation fund — it will drive the growth of small businesses that will take our research and turn it into tools that farmers can use, and it will also create a community of farmers that know how technology can be used on their farms."
_— Dr. Christina Grozinger, Publius Vergilius Maro Professor of Entomology and Director of The Center for Pollinator Research at Pennsylvania State University_
![Jared Grissinger](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/jared%20grissinger%20cropped)
# Jared Grissinger
**Managing Director, Project & Account Management**
717.214.5313 | jgrissinge@pa.gov
CONNECT (opens in a new tab)
## In the News: PA Agriculture
![Governor Josh Shapiro, standing alongside a group of farmers, speaks at a podium in front of a large silo filled with potatoes.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/26748_gov_racp_26)
## Governor Shapiro invests $3 million in Erie County organic potato company
Governor Josh Shapiro visited start-up company Folkland Foods, located in Waterford, Erie County, to announce a $3 million Redevelopment Assistance Capital Program (RACP) investment in the company. This funding will enable the company to expand its operations, transition more acreage to organic farming, begin producing a range of potato products, and create up to 50 new local jobs in the region over the first three years. Pennsylvania is getting stuff done for agriculture businesses, big and small.
[ READ THE ANNOUNCEMENT](https://pagetsitdone.com/news/governor-shapiro-announces-3-million-investment-in-erie-county-organic-potato-company-to-create-local-jobs-and-grow-pennsylvanias-agricultural-sector)
![Governor Josh Shapiro, standing alongside a group of farmers, speaks at a podium in front of a large silo filled with potatoes.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/26748_gov_racp_26)
![A drone flies over vegetables in a farm, spraying pesticide, during sunset](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_480893444)
## Shapiro Administration announces recipients of the nation’s first Agricultural Innovation Grant
Here in Pennsylvania, we're shaping the future of agriculture through smart investments that reward innovation. Governor Shapiro’s bipartisan Agricultural Innovation Grant Program recently invested in 88 cutting-edge solutions and technologies, which will support agriculture programs in 45 counties across the Commonwealth
[ READ ABOUT THE PROGRAM(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/governor/newsroom/2025-press-releases/shapiro-administration-announces-recipients-of-the-nation-s-firs.html)
##  #1  in Organic Livestock and Poultry Production in the U.S. 
[ U.S. Department of Agriculture  (opens in a new tab)](https://investigatemidwest.org/2023/11/01/graphic-which-states-have-the-most-organic-livestock-and-poultry-farms/)
$13.8 Million in Pennsylvania Farm Bill Investments  [ PA.GOV  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/en/agencies/pda/pa-farm-bill.html)
49,000+  Farms Across the State  [ USDA Census of Agriculture, 2022  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.nass.usda.gov/Publications/AgCensus/2022/Full_Report/Volume_1,_Chapter_1_State_Level/Pennsylvania/)

Check out our interactive data map and learn everything there is to know about agribusiness in Pennsylvania.
[ EXPLORE THE DATA (opens in a new tab)](https://tinyurl.com/7f4ffvxn)
## Funding & Resources
### See some of of the many programs and resources available to agriculture businesses in Pennsylvania.
###  First Industries Fund (FIF)
The First Industries Fund supports Pennsylvania’s agriculture and tourism sectors through low interest loans. These loans can be used for land and building acquisition, construction, machinery, and equipment upgrades.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/first-industries-fund-fif)
###  Agricultural Business Development Center (ABDC)
Established as part of the 2019 PA Farm Bill, the Agricultural Business Development Center (ABDC) supports the long-term vitality of Pennsylvania’s farms, strategic farm expansion, diversification of agricultural production, and offer financial and technical expertise as a resource for the industry. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.agriculture.pa.gov/Business_Industry/Pages/ABDC.aspx)
###  PA Preferred Program
The PA Preferred Program is the official brand of agriculture products made in Pennsylvania. The program promotes agricultural products grown and produced in Pennsylvania as part of public-private partnership between the PA Department of Agriculture and companies. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.agriculture.pa.gov/Business_Industry/pa_preferred/Pages/default.aspx/)
###  PA Food Manufacturers Directory
The PA Department of Agriculture, in partnership with Saint Joseph’s University’s Center for Food Marketing created the PA Food Manufacturers Directory. The database includes Pennsylvania companies that offer food co-packing and private label manufacturing services to help businesses scale up production. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://padeptag.maps.arcgis.com/apps/MapSeries/index.html?appid=0f24bc86da4043e9a9d287fe49bd4748)
###  Pennsylvania Milk Processing Tax Credit Program
The PA EDGE program provides tax credits to expanding businesses in critical manufacturing sectors. The Pennsylvania Milk Processing (PMP) tax credit is available through the PA Department of Revenue. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.revenue.pa.gov/IncentivesCreditsPrograms/PAEDGE/Pages/Milk%20Processing%20Tax%20Credit.aspx)
###  Penn State Extension
Penn State Extension helps individuals, businesses, and communities address problems and realize opportunities through a robust portfolio of educational programs, products, and services. With support from federal, state, and county governments, extension offers unbiased information and science-based support for Pennsylvania’s agriculture industry.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://extension.psu.edu/)

Key Industries
# Manufacturing
![Two manufacturing facility workers pose for a photo while holding a partially-constructed propeller engine.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/lycomingengines_2u2a7830?fmt=webp)
## Engineering the Future of **Manufacturing**
Pennsylvania’s manufacturing industry is an undeniable force. Not only does the sector employ 1 in 10 residents, it contributes more than $111 billion to our state economy each year. With our strong infrastructure and powerful supply of resources, PA is primed for manufacturers looking to scale operations and lead in a competitive market.
Our regions deliver specialized expertise in diverse manufacturing segments. In the Central and Northern regions, plastic product manufacturing integrates seamlessly with the life sciences industry. Metallurgy and metal manufacturing span the state, strengthening robotics, technology, and energy. Meanwhile, our paper product manufacturing continues to evolve and deliver essential materials across sectors. The Commonwealth is [investing $500 million in site development(opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/newsroom/shapiro-administration-opens-400-million-pa-sites-program-to-make-pennsylvania-more-competitive-attract-businesses-and-create-jobs/) to prepare more shovel ready industrial and commercial sites — so companies can get to work, fast. 
We’re also equipping Pennsylvanians with the hands-on skills they need to meet the demands of modern advanced manufacturing. Through initiatives like Manufacturing PA and our cutting-edge apprenticeship and pre-apprenticeship programs, we are preparing the workforce of tomorrow. Since 2023, we’ve secured $23.5 million in workforce development funding and launched the [Commonwealth Workforce Transformation(opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/newsroom/governor-shapiro-signs-executive-order-creating-new-first-in-the-nation-workforce-training-program-to-take-advantage-of-historic-federal-infrastructure-funding/) Program, set to create 10,000 new jobs. In Pennsylvania, manufacturing is more than just an industry; it’s the foundation for a future built on innovation. 
* * *
> We understand that for the U.S. to thrive, more Americans need to work in the high-paying, long-term jobs that manufacturing can provide... it requires a true private-public partnership. That’s why we are so happy to be establishing this operation in New Kensington, where we have been impressed by the commitment of local and state government, educational institutions, RIDC, and local philanthropies... to invest alongside us to build a better future for the local community and our country.”
_- Miles Arnone, CEO, Re: Build Manufacturing (New Kensington)_
![Jared Grissinger](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/jared%20grissinger%20cropped)
# Jared Grissinger
**Managing Director, Project & Account Management**
717.214.5313 | jgrissinge@pa.gov
CONNECT (opens in a new tab)
## In the News: PA Manufacturing
![A rendering of an industrial building near Philadelphia, on a sunny day.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/c11_drinkpak)
## Three reasons why DrinkPAK picked Pennsylvania for its next manufacturing facility
In December 2025, Pennsylvania Governor Josh Shapiro announced that [DrinkPAK(opens in a new tab)](https://www.drinkpak.com/), a canned beverage manufacturer, would be [expanding into the Commonwealth](https://pagetsitdone.com/news/governor-shapiro-secures--195-million-investment-from-drinkpak). Supported by the BusinessPA team and regional economic development partners, DrinkPAK leaders selected a site in Philadelphia’s Bellwether District to construct a new facility that would create 174 jobs and invest $195 million into the region.
[ EXPLORE THE PROJECT](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/manufacturing/case-study-drinkpak)
![Three manufacturing employees wearing shirts with an "East Penn" company logo smile as they work on a modern manufacturing line.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/5008)
## How the world's largest lead battery manufacturer found success in Pennsylvania
Based out of Berks County, East Penn Manufacturing has a rich history of growth in Pennsylvania, and today produces more than 500 types of batteries used in varied commercial and industrial applications worldwide. Their secret to success over the past 80 years? Pennsylvania's people - and the workforce development ecosystem that enables them to find and hire the qualified talent they need.
[ READ THE CASE STUDY](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/manufacturing/case-study--east-penn-manufacturing)
![Three manufacturing employees wearing shirts with an "East Penn" company logo smile as they work on a modern manufacturing line.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/5008)
##  6th Largest  Manufacturing Industry in the U.S. by Employment 
[ U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics, 2025 (opens in a new tab)](https://www.bls.gov/charts/state-employment-and-unemployment/industry-employment-by-state.htm)
$111 Billion  in Gross Domestic Product (GDP) in 2024 [ U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics (opens in a new tab)](https://apps.bea.gov/itable/?ReqID=70)
558,800+  Employees in Manufacturing  [ U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics, 2025 (opens in a new tab)](https://www.bls.gov/regions/mid-atlantic/pennsylvania.htm#eag_pa.f.3)
$30 Million  Increase in CTE Programming and Equipment  [ 2024-25 State Budget  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/governor/newsroom/2024-press-releases/icymi--gov-shapiro-budget-investments-in-higher-education--cte.html#:~:text=$15.7%20million%20increase%20for%20community,state%20funding%20for%20nursing%20apprenticeships)
45 New Apprenticeship Programs (Since January 2023)  [ PA.GOV, 2024  (opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/en/governor/newsroom/2024-press-releases/icymi--gov-shapiro-budget-investments-in-higher-education--cte.html)

## Funding & Resources
### See some of of the many programs and resources available to manufacturing businesses in Pennsylvania.
###  Manufacturing PA Training-to-Career Grant Program
Grants support workforce programs that result in short-term work-readiness training, entry-level job placement, or the advancement of the manufacturing industry.
[ Learn More (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/manufacturing-pa-training-career-grant-program/)
###  Foundations in Industry Training (FIT) Grants
The Foundations in Industry Training (FIT) Grant Program provides Pennsylvania employers with grants to help cover expenses related to instruction complementing on-the-job training. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/foundations-in-industry-training-fit-grant-program/)
###  Manufacturing PA Innovation Program
The Manufacturing PA Innovation Program brings together businesses and internationally acclaimed science and engineering talent and discovery capacity of Pennsylvania’s top research institutions. Undergraduate and graduate student fellows at PA universities work with PA manufacturers to advance new products or process innovations.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/manufacturing-pa-innovation-program/)
###  WEDnetPA
WEDnetPA provides employers with training funds for new and existing employees. It’s a unique, collaborative partnership between community colleges, state system universities, and other educational institutions working together to respond to the evolving needs of Pennsylvania’s business community. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/wednetpa/)
###  Ben Franklin Technology Partners (BFTP)
The BFTP are a national model for technology-based economic development programs. BFTP provides both early-stage, technology-based firms and established manufacturers with funding, business and technical expertise, and access to a network of innovative, expert resources.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://benfranklin.org/)
###  Regional Clean Hydrogen Hubs Tax Credit Program
The PA EDGE program provides tax credits to expanding businesses in critical manufacturing sectors. Manufacturers purchasing clean hydrogen and natural gas from a Regional Clean Hydrogen Hub (RCHH) many qualify for tax credits through the PA Department of Revenue.
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.revenue.pa.gov/IncentivesCreditsPrograms/PAEDGE/Pages/Regional-Clean-Hydrogen-Hubs-Tax-Credit.aspx)
###  Industrial Resource Centers (IRC)
The Industrial Resource Centers are a network of seven private, nonprofits located strategically throughout the state to provide localized support. The network works with manufacturers to respond to changing market conditions, adopt new technology, and on creating strategies to remain competitive in today’s global economy.
[ Learn More (opens in a new tab)](https://pamade.org/)
###  NextManufacturing Center
The NextManufacturing Center at Carnegie Mellon University is one of the world’s leading research centers for additive manufacturing. The Center offers workforce training in collaboration with local nonprofits to capitalize on the abundance of manufacturing employers in southwestern Pennsylvania. The Center also offers the only undergraduate Additive Manufacturing course in the country.
[ Learn More (opens in a new tab)](https://engineering.cmu.edu/next/index.html)

Locate or Expand
# Development & Expansion **Support**
![An industrial, modern office space with a few people mingling in the background](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/4%20pcenter%20perch?fmt=webp)
## **New Opportunities Await** Growing Businesses
Are you looking to expand or relocate your business in PA? The **BusinessPA Team** is ready to assist you in implementing your business growth strategy.
Pennsylvania has a [strategic location](https://pagetsitdone.com/why-pa/location_and_infrastructure "Locate or Expand"), a [world-class workforce](https://pagetsitdone.com/why-pa/workforce "Workforce"), and an excellent mix of [affordability and quality of life](https://pagetsitdone.com/why-pa/quality_of_life "Link to Quality of Life page") that makes it the best place on the East Coast to do business. Combined with a business-friendly tax environment in which our corporate net income tax rate is on a path to 4.99 percent – among the lowest in the nation – we are confident that the next location for your business should be right here in the Keystone State.
Take a closer look at Pennsylvania and give the BusinessPA Team a call at **717.787.8199.** You can also explore the map below for contact information for professional staff in each of our regional offices and for staff in our headquarters in Harrisburg.
Are you a small business owner? We've got you covered. Dedicated resources and support are available at our [Business One-Stop Shop website.](https://business.pa.gov/)
![Michael O'Rourke](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1738506522244)
## **Mike O'Rourke**
Managing Director, Business Retention & Expansion
CONNECT 
## Looking for a local connection?
**In addition to our Harrisburg headquarters, the BusinessPA team has representatives at each of our regional offices. If you have a question about specific sites, regional programs, local partners, or general inquiries at the county/city level, we encourage you to connect with us!**
Use arrow keys to choose tabs. Content for the chosen tab will be revealed below.

# About **BusinessPA**
![Michael O'Rourke is interviewed by two videographers at an outdoor event at SXSW. A food truck and crowd are visible in the distance.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/sxsw_michael_fullres-1?fmt=webp)
## We're **Getting Stuff Done**
Pennsylvania is a place where big ideas can achieve even bigger success, and where businesses can grow and prosper. More importantly — you don't have to do it alone. Our BusinessPA team is your dedicated partner for growth. We are committed to providing individualized and responsive support to businesses like yours. Whether you're looking to relocate to the Commonwealth, expand your workforce here, tap into global markets, or something else entirely, our team is available to assist at every stage of the process.
So, what does this new BusinessPA  
  
Meet our team below, and dive into our 10-year Economic Development Strategy to get to know our vision for business success across the Commonwealth.
> We’re grateful for Governor Shapiro’s administration and all of our state and local partners for their support, which is enabling small companies like ours to invest in equipment and expand production."
_- Joseph Wolf, CEO,[**Powerex, Inc.**(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pwrx.com/ "Link to Powerex website") (Youngwood)_
![Secretary Rick Siger](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/rick_siger-1)
## Secretary Rick Siger
PA Department of Community & Economic Development
![A rendering of a document. The cover says: "A Ten-Year Strategic Plan for Economic Development in Pennsylvania."](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/econdevstrategy_digitalcover-final-copy-1-2048x1909-1)
## A strategy that's **driving success**
In 2024, Governor Josh Shapiro announced a bold vision for economic prosperity in the Commonwealth—Pensylvana's first new Economic Development strategy in two decades. We're already executing this ambitious ten-year plan, which serves as our agency's blueprint for investing in economic growth.
By prioritizing strategic investments in our key industries, continuing to make government work at the speed of business, creating an ecosystem that rewards innovation, and building vibrant and resilient regions, we're creating real opportunities for our businesses, communities, and residents.
[ DOWNLOAD THE STRATEGY](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/documents/economicdevelopmentstrategy-dced_2024_final.pdf)
![A rendering of a document. The cover says: "A Ten-Year Strategic Plan for Economic Development in Pennsylvania."](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/econdevstrategy_digitalcover-final-copy-1-2048x1909-1)
![Michael O'Rourke](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1738506522244)
## **Mike O'Rourke**
Managing Director, Business Retention & Expansion

#  Growth happens**in Pennsylvania**
![A group of employees wearing shirts with the logo for the company Kettle and Fire cut a ceremonial ribbon outside a new manufacturing building](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/kettle%20and%20fire%20ribbon%20cutting?fmt=webp)
## Do Business Here.
## **Unlock Opportunities.**
## The BusinessPA team is ready to help you implement your business growth strategy.
Pennsylvania has the [strategic location, world-class workforce, and excellent mix of affordability and quality of life](https://pagetsitdone.com/why-pa "Link to the Why PA page on the Pennsylvania Gets It Done site.") that makes it the best place on the East Coast to do business. Combined with a business-friendly tax environment in which our corporate net income tax rate is on a path to 4.99 percent – among the lowest in the nation – and we are confident that the next location for your business should be right here in the Keystone State.
Take a closer look at what Pennsylvania has to offer and call the BusinessPA Team at 717.787.8199, or visit our [Development and Expansion](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/development_and_expansion_support "Link to Development and Expansion page") page to find regional office staff contacts. Have a question? [Contact us via our webform](https://pagetsitdone.com/contact_us "Link to Contact Us page"), and we'll connect you with the right people, programs, and resources to help your business grow.
![A man walks through an industrial office space](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/4%20pcenter%20perch)
## Development & Expansion Support
Whether you're a domestic company looking to move your company's operations to Pennsylvania, or an existing Commonwealth company taking the next steps to expand your presence here, we have people and programs ready to support your ambitions.
[ EXPLORE DEVELOPMENT SUPPORT](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/development_and_expansion_support)
![Aerial image of industial buildings and land](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Glassworks%20Site%20compressed)
## Sites & Incentives
In 2024 alone, the Commonwealth invested a staggering $500 million on site development programs, including $400 million toward [PA SITES(opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/pennsylvania-strategic-investments-to-enhance-sites-program-pa-sites/), a program that supports companies with funds for planning and construction. We also offer incentives for site redevelopment, projects in targeted economic development zones, and so much more. Read on to see the ways we're making it easy to make your next move right here in Pennsylvania.
[ EXPLORE SITES & INCENTIVES](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/sites_and_incentives)
![Aerial image of industial buildings and land](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Glassworks%20Site%20compressed)
![BioLab technicians work in a lab, surrounded by scientific equipment](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/3%20pcenter%20lab)
## Foreign Direct Investment (FDI)
More than than 5,600 foreign-owned companies operate in Pennsylvania, and the list is growing — for good reason. With a diverse economy that spans industries from agriculture to advanced technology, and a GDP rivaling the size of most countries, PA is an ideal place for international companies looking to relocate or expand in the U.S. 
[ EXPLORE FDI](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment)
![A forklift loads trucks with packages at a shipping and logistics center](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_437939719)
## International Trade
Received a trade lead from another country and need export assistance? Having trouble finding a qualified partner in a new market? Wrestling with foreign regulations to get your product into a new market? We offer a wide range of programs and services to help you address these and many other international business challenges. Learn more about trading from and with Pennsylvania, and connect with regional experts who can help you get it done.
[ EXPLORE INTERNATIONAL TRADE](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/trade)
![A forklift loads trucks with packages at a shipping and logistics center](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_437939719)
![Michael O'Rourke](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1738506522244)
## **Mike O'Rourke**
Managing Director, Business Retention & Expansion
CONNECT (opens in a new tab)
## We want your business here in PA.
Looking for specialized help? Get in touch with our subject matter experts!

Key Industries
# Robotics & **Technology**
![A man holding a laptop controls a humanoid, white plastic robot in a warehouse-like space](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/cmuroboticsinstitute2?fmt=webp)
## Where Technology and Robotics Shape **What's Next**
Welcome to the birthplace of artificial intelligence and a global hub for robotics.
Pennsylvania’s pioneering legacy is closely linked to [Carnegie Mellon University](https://www.cmu.edu/), where the field of AI was invented and the world’s first doctoral program in robotics was founded. Today, companies across the state are trailblazing innovations in autonomous vehicles, space exploration, advanced manufacturing, precision medicine, and beyond.
Home to two of the nation’s top 10 universities for robotics, Pennsylvania is a magnet for top talent in the field. Companies here benefit from cutting-edge R&D institutions, a strong network of venture capital opportunities, and billions of dollars in federal funding through the CHIPS Act, Bipartisan Infrastructure Law, and Inflation Reduction Act. We’re staying ahead of the curve to build breakthrough technologies that will redefine industries.
Companies like Pittsburgh’s [Astrobotic](https://www.astrobotic.com/) are already proving that in the Commonwealth, the sky’s not the limit — it’s just the beginning. With [$4 million in state funding](https://dced.pa.gov/newsroom/shapiro-administration-invests-millions-in-astrobotic-technology-helping-the-leading-space-and-robotics-company-expand-and-create-nearly-300-high-tech-jobs-ahead-of-december-moon-launch/) to expand their headquarters, they’re leading innovation in space robotics for lunar and planetary missions. The next decade in Pennsylvania promises even more growth, with nearly 17,000 net new jobs projected across our robotics and technology industries. Bring your business here to push the boundaries of possibility. 
* * *
> “We’re using robotics and software to help change the way critical industries like defense, manufacturing, and energy production build and operate. And none of that would have been possible without the unique ecosystem we have in western PA. We have a huge opportunity to build an unstoppable economic engine, bringing government and entrepreneurs together to solve real-world problems.” 
_— Jake Loosararian, Co-founder and CEO, Gecko Robotics (Pittsburgh)_
![Jared Grissinger](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/jared%20grissinger%20cropped)
# Jared Grissinger
**Managing Director, Project & Account Management**
717.214.5313 | jgrissinge@pa.gov
CONNECT 
## In the News: PA Robotics
![A rendering of a small robot climbing up the siding of an industrial surface. A decorative illustration of a computer program monitoring the robots activities is visible.](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/key-industries/robotics/2f8f49affb49a2028a2e76c7fc729bf29b60f3c9-2721x1609.jpg)
## Pittsburgh-based Gecko Robotics a shining example of PA's thriving robotics ecosystem
[Gecko Robotics](https://www.geckorobotics.com/) is a national leader in using robotics and software to build, operate, and maintain the world’s most important physical infrastructure and was recently named to Fast Company’s list of the [World’s Most Innovative Companies](https://www.fastcompany.com/91039216/robotics-most-innovative-companies-2024 "Link to Fast Company article") of 2024. Pennsylvania has supported Gecko’s growth over the last decade, seeding it with [$10,000 from Ben Franklin Technology Partners](https://ecenterlindenpointe.com/ben-franklin-technology-partners-seed-investment-will-help-gecko-robotics/ "Link to ECenter Linden website") in 2014 to help co-founder Jake Loosararian build one of the company's first robots.
[ READ THE ANNOUNCEMENT](https://pagetsitdone.com/news/governor-shapiro-tours-gecko-robotics-in-pittsburgh-highlights-how-economic-development-strategy-and-proposed-budget-investments-will-strengthen-pennsylvanias-growing-innovation-economy)
![A rendering of a small robot climbing up the siding of an industrial surface. A decorative illustration of a computer program monitoring the robots activities is visible.](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/key-industries/robotics/2f8f49affb49a2028a2e76c7fc729bf29b60f3c9-2721x1609.jpg)
![Astrobotic employees show off a robotic arm prototype in their facility to Gov. Josh Shapiro and cohorts.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/24064_gov_astrobotics_06)
## Shapiro Administration invests millions in Astrobotic Technology, helping the space and robotics company expand
[Astrobotic](https://www.astrobotic.com/) — a Pittsburgh-based robotics company working with NASA on technology for planned lunar missions — received $4.38 million in investments fron the Shapiro Administration to help the company expand. Astrobotic is renovating a new $20 million "space campus" that will create 283 new, high-tech jobs and retain 174 employees and currently boasts over 180 Pennsylvania suppliers. 
[ READ THE ANNOUNCEMENT](https://dced.pa.gov/newsroom/shapiro-administration-invests-millions-in-astrobotic-technology-helping-the-leading-space-and-robotics-company-expand-and-create-nearly-300-high-tech-jobs-ahead-of-december-moon-launch/)
##  #1  AI Program in the U.S. (Carnegie Mellon University) 
[ U.S. News & World Report, 2025  ](https://www.usnews.com/best-colleges/rankings/computer-science/artificial-intelligence)
2 of the Top 10 Universities for Robotics  [ EduRank, 2024  ](https://edurank.org/engineering/robotics/us/)
17,000  Net New Jobs Projected Across Robotics & Tech Sectors  [ PA ECONOMIC DEVELOPMENT STRATEGY, 2024 ](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/documents/economicdevelopmentstrategy-dced_2024_final.pdf)
$3.12 Billion Raised by Pittsburgh Tech Economy in 2023  [ Pittsburgh Inno, 2023  ](https://www.bizjournals.com/pittsburgh/inno/stories/news/2024/03/20/report-finds-tech-economy-funding.html)

## Funding & Resources
### See some of of the many programs and resources available to robotics and technology businesses in Pennsylvania.
###  Ben Franklin Technology Partners (BFTP)
The BFTP are a national model for technology-based economic development programs. BFTP provides both early-stage, technology-based firms and established manufacturers with funding, business and technical expertise, and access to a network of innovative, expert resources.
[ Learn More ](https://benfranklin.org/)
###  Penn Center for Innovation
University of Pennsylvania’s Penn Center for Innovation facilitates technology transfer from university research to the private sector through licensing, R&D alliances, and other commercial partnering opportunities. Opportunities exist in a broad range of sectors, including nanotechnology, electronic materials, robotics, computer information systems, bioengineering, medical devices, and more. 
[ LEARN MORE ](https://pci.upenn.edu/)
###  Pittsburgh Robotics Network (PRN)
The Pittsburgh Robotics Network connects industry with robotics leaders, and stakeholders to accelerate opportunities for business growth and the adoption of robotic solutions and artificial intelligence technologies.
[ LEARN MORE ](https://robopgh.org/about)
###  National Robotics Engineering Center (NREC)
Operating within the CMU Robotics Institute, the National Robotics Engineering Center (NREC) is a technology transfer organization that designs, develops, and tests robotic systems and vehicles for industrial and government clients. The NREC combines systems engineering disciplines of requirements and trades analysis, design, simulation, integration and testing with applied research capabilities in autonomy, sensing and unmanned platform design. The NREC excels in rapid integration and field-testing of automated systems and several of their systems have transitioned to industry and the military.
[ LEARN MORE ](https://www.nrec.ri.cmu.edu/nrec/)
###  Advanced Robotics for Manufacturing Institute (ARM)
The ARM Institute is a public-private partnership bringing together more than 300 organizations across industry, government, and academia to drive the use of industrial robots to strengthen the U.S. manufacturing sector. Key industrial sectors include aerospace, automotive, electronics, and textiles. 
[ LEARN MORE ](https://arminstitute.org/)
###  Industrial Resource Centers (IRC)
The Industrial Resource Centers are a network of seven private, nonprofits located strategically throughout the state to provide localized support. The network works with manufacturers to respond to changing market conditions, adopt new technology, and on creating strategies to remain competitive in today’s global economy. 
[ LEARN MORE ](https://pamade.org/find-your-regional-irc/)

Foreign Direct Investment
#  International **Success Stories**
![A group of businesspeople pose for a picture in an office space with interior windows and a blue wall](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Reykjavik%20Creamery?fmt=webp)
## Home to the World's **Best and Brightest** Global Companies
Today, more than 5,600 foreign-owned firms employing over 324,000 workers have business operations in Pennsylvania. Countries leading in foreign investment include the United Kingdom, Germany, France, Japan, Switzerland, and Canada. We also have a growing number of Brazilian, Korean, Israeli, and Chinese firms here. It’s a list that’s growing — and for good reason! Here in Pennsylvania, we actively support the companies looking to expand here - and the success stories speak for themselves.
* * *
##  Notable Global Companies in PA 
[ ![Greiner company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/fdi/fdi-success-stories/csm_greiner-packaging_rgb_a3ba649772.png) (opens in a new tab)](https://www.greiner-gpi.com/en)
[ ![Infosys](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/company-logos/infosys-logo.png) (opens in a new tab)](https://www.infosys.com/)
[ ![Almac Group](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/company-logos/int_sm_almac.png) (opens in a new tab)](https://www.almacgroup.com/)
[ ![B. Braun company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/company-logos/bbraun-resized.png) (opens in a new tab)](https://www.bbraunusa.com/en.html)
[ ![SAP company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/company-logos/sap_2011_logo.svg.png) (opens in a new tab)](https://www.sap.com/index.html)
* * *
## International Companies are Growing in PA.
## Read their stories - then make your move.
![Executives speak at a podium in a conference room, with balloons in the background.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Salaet%20Group%20Photo)
## Salaet Invests $7 Million in Pennsylvania for U.S Headquarters
Spanish food packaging company [Salaet](https://www.linkedin.com/company/salaet-foodpackaging/) picked Pennsylvania for its first U.S. headquarters, investing $7 million and creating 35 jobs in the process. Discover why this company decided that Wayne County was the perfect place to set up shop.
[ READ SALAET CASE STUDY](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment/fdi_success_stories/success_story_salaet)
![Executives speak at a podium in a conference room, with balloons in the background.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Salaet%20Group%20Photo)
![A rendering of an industrial building near Pittsburgh, on a sunny day.](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/fdi/fdi-success-stories/bgs.jpg)
## BGS Chooses Pennsylvania for First U.S. Facility
Medical products used by hospitals and healthcare providers across the United States often undergo a sterlization process before distribution, and BGS Beta-Gamma-Service saw an opportunity to bring their technology and services to the U.S. market. Discover what brought them to PA and the advantages they found doing business here.
[ READ BGS CASE STUDY](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment/fdi_success_stories/success_story_bgs)
![Two men in business attire smile for a photo, standing in front of a large warehouse. The warehouse has a logo for the company Easy Signs on it, and cars are parked in front of the building.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/es_outsidefactory)
## Easy Signs Grows in U.S. with Lehigh Valley Manufacturing Facility
After experiencing increased sales to the United States, Easy Signs decided to open a manufacturing facility stateside to produce high quality, digitally printed signage. Discover more about the project which is estimated to create 130 jobs over three years in Allentown.
[ READ EASY SIGNS CASE STUDY](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment/fdi_success_stories/success_story_easy-signs)
![Two men in business attire smile for a photo, standing in front of a large warehouse. The warehouse has a logo for the company Easy Signs on it, and cars are parked in front of the building.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/es_outsidefactory)
##  Over 20 Companies Supported by BusinessPA International Team in FY23-24 
$91.6 Million Business Investments Pledged in FY23-24 by FDI Companies
330 Jobs to be Created by FDI Expansion Projects in FY23-24
![Men in suits discuss business near international flags](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_340862015)
## **WE CAN HELP YOU GROW IN NEW GLOBAL MARKETS**
BusinessPA's International team offers customized services to help international companies looking to locate or expand in our state. Our [global investment representatives](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment/global_investment_reps.html) serve as business advocates and liaisons between potential foreign investors and BusinessPA. We're connecting you with PA companies to create mutually beneficial partnerships while eliminating barriers so you can invest, expand, and operate your business with ease in Pennsylvania. **Here's just a glimpse of what we do every day:**
  * Helping you set up a U.S. business entity
  * Identifying and visiting business sites
  * In-depth research on available workforce, infrastructure, taxes, and more
  * Introductions to regional and local economic development partners and elected officials
  * Customized financial assistance — including grants, low– interest loans, tax credits, bond financing, and job training


![Men in suits discuss business near international flags](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_340862015)
> By relocating hydraulic valve production from China to the U.S., we are not only investing in domestic manufacturing, but also strengthening our supply chain, reducing delivery times, creating jobs, and supporting the local economy."
_Mike Kozak, General Manager, Hawe Manufacturing U.S., Inc. (Lehigh Valley)_

# Global Investment **Representatives**
![A group of businessmen and businesswomen cut a ribbon and smile for a photo in a brightly lit atrium](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/hydro_ribbon_cutting?fmt=webp)
## A Global Team that **Speaks Your Language**
Pennsylvania’s global investment representatives serve as business advocates and liaisons between potential foreign investors and BusinessPA. These representatives are committed to supporting international companies and eliminating the barriers that foreign companies might encounter while investing, expanding, or operating a business in Pennsylvania.
Get in touch with the [designated representative for your country(opens in a new tab)](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/documents/direct%20investment_contact%20insert-2025v4.pdf) or region below.

Foreign Direct Investment
# Frequently **Asked** Questions
![A Pennsylvania street sign in front of a historic building on a sunny day](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_593125044?fmt=webp)
If you're considering expanding your business operations to Pennsylvania (an excellent idea!), we understand that there are a lot of things to consider - from tax implications to labor laws that may differ from other places. We've collected many of our most-asked questions here - but if you don't see your question listed, please don't hesitate to contact our [International team](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment "Link to Interational Investments team") or your [regional representative](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/foreign_direct_investment/global_investment_reps "Link to Regional Representatives page") for additional assistance.
