###  SPP108 | Steel
Italy
Automated material handling equipment for the Steel Industry
**SIC:** 3536 – 3537 – 5084
**NAICS:** N/A
**Main Product(s):** This company is a well-established Italian company that specializes in the design, manufacture, and installation of highly-automated technologies for the Steel industry. Such products include: automatic guided vehicles (AGV) for coils logistic, automated overhead cranes, automated Warehouse Management Systems and all the other rail-bound integrated solutions for complex material handling. This company has decades of experience working with all the major Steel producers, such as Arcelor Mittal, with projects all over Italy and Europe and is widely recognized as a specialized supplier of tailor-made material handling solutions in the steel industry.
The Italian company is looking to acquire a company which currently supplies equipment to the steel industry. The ideal partner would have a recognized brand and clients among steel manufacturers, and would be looking for an infusion of capital and automation design/build experience. This company is open to considering different forms of partnership. Their vision is to create an entity in the United States which can design and build customized automation solutions for the steel industry, and provide after-sales service and maintenance to their customers.
###  SPP141 | Machine Manufacturing
India
Casting/machining, precision iron and aluminum parts
**SIC:** 3544
**NAICS:** 332721
**Main Product(s):** This company has been in the business of casting & machining very high-precision iron and aluminum parts since 1982. The complementary products include but are not limited to Agricultural Implements and farm Equipment, Pumps for applications such as Water Applications (for domestic use), Industrial (pulp & paper industry, petroleum & gas, etc), and Firefighting pumps and Automotive applications (components & assemblies). The company supplies components & assemblies to some of the most reputed companies in the fields of Farm engines (SAME DEUTZ-FAHR, Mitsubishi Diesel Engines, Mahindra & Mahindra), pumps (Grundfos, Ebara, Andritz) and general engineering (PSG Dover, LMW). This is a very successful company in Europe looking to expand in the US in partnership with a PA company. In addition to capital investment into the JV, they bring this experience of manufacturing and supply chain management to the table”. Ideal partner is described as:
  1. a company engaged in manufacturing complementary products and would like to expand its operations/product line
  2. Preferably a mid-size family-owned company that shares similar values of trust, commitment, and long-term approach towards business development.


Established 1982.
###  SPP144 | Packaging
Australia
Manufacturing
**SIC:** 3565
**NAICS:** 333993
**Main Product(s):** Established in 2007, this Australian manufacturer of quality packaging machinery (liquid filling machines, labelers, cappers, printers, etc.) is seeking to identify a suitable partner in the US to assist them in growing their business in that market. The company primarily services the FMCG market, across the Food & Bev, Cosmetics & Beauty, Pharmaceuticals & Veterinary, and Industrial & Chemical sectors, and is also Australia’s largest sales, rental & technical services provider to the FMCG packaging sector.
The company is now seeking to partner with a US company to assist them with expansion into the North American market. An ideal partner will have:
  * experience operating in the packaging and manufacturing space, particularly FMCG
  * a least one warehouse for operations to receive and unpack equipment
  * a technical/operations team that can unpack, deliver, and install the machinery
  * a fully functioning business unit that is self-sufficient i.e., sales, marketing, finance, technical, operations etc


###  SPP151 | Casting
Italy
Alloys Production
**SIC:** 2444420
**NAICS:** N/A
**Main Product(s):** Established in 2004, this company has forty years of experience in the production of light alloys, series – EN AB 41. 000, 42. 000, 43. 000, 44. 000, 45. 000, 51. 000 and 71. 000). They have expertise in the aluminum, magnesium and melting processes in shell, sand and die casting. The company is looking to expand their US footprint/client base and are seeking a suitable partner in Pennsylvania to assist them in their North American market growth goals. Partners can include companies in the aerospace, defense and automotive sectors/industries and/or a company with synergy of product.
###  SPP154 | Consumer Goods
Turkey
Manufacturing
**SIC** : N/A
**NAICS** : N/A
**Main Product(s):** This company is the largest manufacturer of nonwoven/woven reusable bags in Europe and the market and a leader in sustainable carrier bag solutions in Turkey. Additionally, the company designs and manufactures cutting machines used in the production of these bags.
**Target Partner:** The company is interested in establishing a scalable and sustainable growth model by building a local partnership with regional distributorships and joint venture to accelerate market adaptation in the US. They also wish to establish a production facility in the US by building a broader export and sales network.
###  SPP157 | Springs
Germany
Manufacturing
**SIC** : N/A
**NAICS** : 332613, 332322, 332999
**Main Product(s):** Founded in 1990, this German manufacturer produces a variety of springs for the electrical engineering, healthcare and advanced manufacturing industries. Their product range comprises several types of springs made from spring or stainless steel or steel wire such as shaped springs, box springs, punched and bend parts, laser cut parts and spring clips. 
**Target Partner:** They have about 100 employees and are aiming to grow and increase their presence in the US. Therefore, they are looking for an American manufacturer ranging in size from 50-300 employees with similar capabilities that is able to produce most of, if not the entire product range. An existing ISO 9001 certification would be ideal.
###  SPP160 | Lab Equipment
Poland
Lab Equipment
**SIC** : 3821
**NAICS** : 334516
**Project Description:** A Polish manufacturer of laboratory equipment is seeking a strategic partnership with an after-sales service provider who could facilitate distribution. Founded in 1990, the Polish company manufactures laboratory and environmental testing equipment such as Drying ovens, incubators, sterilizers, constant climatic chambers, and CO2 incubators. The company has a distribution network in over 100 countries worldwide and is interested in expanding into the North American market through a strategic partnership with a laboratory products maintenance supplier. The company is also interested in exploring distribution networks in North America through the partnership.
Through user-friendly displays and its LabDesk software that allows users to monitor and control devices through Ethernet, USB, or Wifi, the company applies high-quality and innovative R&D to its products. A mobile version of the LabDesk Cloud application is also available for download from the App Store and Google Play. The company is looking to onboard technical staff who will provide basic support to end users as well as a sales team trained by existing staff in Poland if the potential partner does not have experience in distribution. Warehousing is not required.
###  SPP167 | Consumer Goods
Spain
Manufacturing
**SIC** : 3842
**NAICS** : 339113
**Project Description:** A Spanish manufacturer of walkers and complementary mobility products is seeking a Pennsylvania-based co-manufacturer to produce and distribute their products in the North American market. The company currently sells their product through e-commerce platforms but is looking to streamline their supply chain by manufacturing and distributing their products through a subcontract. The ideal partner should have experience in the industry and background distributing to orthopedic retailers and specialized centers where walkers are sold. No specific licenses are required.
###  SPP169 | Vehicles
Spain
Consumer Products
**SIC** : N/A
**NAICS** : TBC
**Project Description:** This Spanish company established in 1860 manufactures motorhome bodies including trailers and semi-trailers. The company is interested in exploring a joint venture partnership with a Pennsylvanian modular/mobile-home manufacturer preferably with in-house engineering expertise and experience adapting RVs and motorhomes to U.S. regulatory requirements. In addition to manufacturing, the ideal partner will also be able to conduct after-sale maintenance and has a developed distribution network in the United States and North America.
###  SPP171 | Defense & Heavy Manufacturing
Australia
Defense & Heavy Manufacturing
**SIC** : 3312
**NAICS** : 331110
**Project Description:** Established in 1980, a publicly listed Australian steel manufacturing company is seeking a strategic partnership and/or a joint venture with a Pennsylvania company already embedded in the US defense, heavy manufacturing, or advanced materials sector, with established customer networks within the defense industry and the credibility to accelerate the company’s U.S. market presence. The company leads Australia’s manufacturing of armor-grade quenched and tempered (Q&T) steel plate. While the initial focus on US market entry is on armor-grade steels for ballistic protection, there is a willingness to explore the option to supply high-strength structural and wear-resistant steels to sectors including mining, energy, transport, and heavy engineering.
The company is interested in exploring a strategic partnership that facilitates technology transfer or co-development opportunities and is open to exploring longer-term arrangements through shared investment or joint operational models. To reflect scale and commitment, the company sees target market volumes of 10,000 metric tons per year into the defense sector after three years of development and growth. The ideal Pennsylvania-based partner should possess certified quality systems (e.g. ISO 9001, AS9100, or defense-specific accreditation), demonstrated experience supplying to U.S. defense primes or integrators, and a proven track record in handling specialty metals or amor-related components. Additionally, strong logistics capacity, including heat-treating, cutting, machining, and finishing capabilities, would be considered highly desirable, along with the ability to support scalable production. However, there are no pre-conceived constraints on partner scale, location, or structure.
###  SPP177 | Enterprise Resource Planning
Portugal
Enterprise Resource Planning
**SIC** : 7373
**NAICS** : 541511
**Project Description:** RAILES is an AI-driven Manufacturing Execution System (MES) designed to orchestrate and optimize industrial operations in highly regulated environments such as pharmaceutical and defense manufacturing. The platform connects machines, operators, and management in real time, providing full visibility and control over production performance.  
  
RAILES leverages artificial intelligence to analyze factory data, support operational decision-making, and continuously improve efficiency. Key capabilities include an AI-powered assistant for operators that provides contextual recommendations on how to run the plant, as well as a digital twin that enables advanced simulations without interfering with live production.  
  
The product is developed by a Portuguese technology company established in 2015, specializing in high-tech software solutions for regulated industries.  
  
The company is currently seeking an implementation partner in Pennsylvania to deliver RAILES MES locally. Implementation will require at least six new jobs including a project manager and five technicians. The ideal partner will have proven experience with MES implementations and a strong track record with pharmaceutical and defense industry clients. Following the initial rollout, the company aims to establish a local presence in Pennsylvania and is open to exploring long-term partnership models.
###  SPP149 | Coffee
Kenya
Coffee
**SIC:** 2095
**NAICS:** 311920
**Project Description:** A family-owned Kenyan specialty coffee company with farming roots dating back to 1954, offering direct-origin access to high-quality Kenyan Arabica coffee. The company supplies a range of graded coffees, including AA, AB, and other specialty and commercial classifications, available in both green and roasted formats.
With deep ties to production and sourcing, the company maintains a strong focus on quality consistency, traceability, and reliable supply at commercial scale. As a licensed coffee dealer, it is well-positioned to support established partners seeking dependable access to Kenyan-origin coffee.
The company is seeking to partner with a Pennsylvania-based coffee roaster and/or specialty beverage company with existing roasting and distribution capabilities. The objective is to establish a long-term, direct supply relationship that enhances supply chain efficiency into the U.S. East Coast market.
This partnership is designed to support value-added activity in Pennsylvania through local roasting, distribution, and potential warehousing, while providing partners with a consistent and strategically sourced coffee supply. The company is open to long-term agreements and collaborative market development initiatives.
###  SPP152 | Preservatives
France
Food Production
**SIC** : 2038
**NAICS** : N/A
**Main Product(s):** This family-owned company was established in 1942 and are a worldwide leader of fruit purees for pastries, restaurants, and bars. To support their expansion/growth in the U.S., the company is looking for a co-manufacturer partner to make their products in the U.S.
The company will invest the CAPEX for the process/equipment and will purchase raw materials and packaging. The partner will supply an available surface of minimum 15,000 square feet for the process and equipment, will stock raw materials and finished products and will supply labor and utilities. Looking for a partner with synergy of product.
###  SPP156 | Frozen Products
France
Food Manufacturing
**SIC:** 2037-02
**NAICS:** 311412
**Overview:** The partner is a French food company manufacturing premium ready-made products and premium frozen potatoes products, currently generates a turnover of €300 million. The company currently owns four industrial factories in France and employs more than 600 employees. While all food manufacturing is done in France, roughly 20% of its activities are carried out in the United States. As a result, the company is aiming to grow and increase their customer base in North America through a joint venture with a US-based firm. The company is interesting in partnering with a US food processing firm that has experience with frozen ready-made products and capacity and capabilities to produce most of, if not all, the entire product range.
###  SPP177 | Yogurt
France
Yogurt
**SIC:** 2099
**NAICS:** 311988
**Project Description:** A family-owned French dairy company is interested in exploring a licensing partnership to manufacture and distribute dairy-alternative products under its own brand. As the market for plant-based products continues to grow and consumers are growing more interested in healthier and environmentally friendly alternatives, the company, which has EUR 310 million in annual revenue, is seeking to establish a foothold in Pennsylvania to meet this need.
The ideal partner would be a mid- to large-sized dairy or yogurt manufacturing company is interested in expanding into the plant-based space.
###  SPP174 | Consumer Products
Australia
Consumer Products
**SIC:** 8731
**NAICS:** 541715
**Project Description:** An established Australian life sciences company has developed a proprietary, non-steroidal topical therapy targeting inflammatory dermatological conditions, including eczema. The formulation addresses a significant unmet need in the US market, where long-term steroid use presents clinical and consumer challenges. The company has assembled a strong pre-commercial evidence base and is now progressing towards North American regulatory and market entry milestones. The company is seeking collaboration with a Pennsylvania-based academic medical center or research institution to support the next phase of clinical and regulatory development with a focus on clinical study design and execution aligned to US regulatory expectations.
The ideal partner for this project would be an academic or research institution with recognized dermatology or translational medicine capability. The partner should have proven experience supporting clinical validation for topical or consumer health products and interest in industry collaboration with potential for sponsored research, co-publication, or longer-term translational engagement. The overall goal of this project is to generate data to support product distribution and US retail pathways.
###  SPP175 | Consumer Products
Australia
Consumer Products
**SIC:** 8731
**NAICS:** 541715
**Project Description:** An Australian life sciences company with a differentiated, non-steroidal dermatology product is preparing for entry into the US consumer and professional healthcare markets. Initial demand modelling supports a staged approach beginning with contract manufacturing and distribution. The company seeks Pennsylvania-based partners across manufacturing and supply chain functions to enable compliant, efficient US market entry. The ideal partner would be a pharmaceutical or medical product contract manufacturer with established distribution networks and capabilities to package and label products. Additional requirements include GMP-compliance and 3PL providers with familiarity of regulated consumer health or OTC products.
## Check back soon!
###  SPP149 | Fertilizer
Lithuania
Manufacturing
**SIC:** N/A
**NAICS:** N/A
**Main Product(s):** Established in 1994, this company manufactures an organic fertilizer using a unique process and product. They are looking to expand their US footprint/client base and are seeking a suitable partner in Pennsylvania to assist them in their North American market growth goals. Partners can include garden centers, industrial farmers, stakeholders in the agronomy market, etc.
###  SPP166 | Artificial Intelligence
Israel
Emergency Management
**SIC:** N/A
**NAICS:** 541519
**Overview:** MdaNet is a next-generation emergency management and response platform developed by a leading Israeli emergency organization. The system integrates artificial intelligence (AI), Internet of Things (IoT), and cloud-based technologies to coordinate emergency operations across medical, fire, and disaster-response networks. Its suite includes real-time vehicle analytics, remote monitoring systems, AI-assisted dispatch, and automated supply and defibrillator cabinets, all managed through a centralized web and mobile interface.
MdaNet’s technology has been field-proven to reduce response times, enhance coordination, and automate critical decision-making across complex emergency environments. The company is now seeking strategic partners in the United States—beginning in Pennsylvania—to scale and localize deployment. Ideal partners include established players in emergency response, healthcare systems, or connected mobility with a strong operational track record and an interest in digital transformation.
MdaNet welcomes joint ventures, licensing agreements, or co-deployment opportunities with EMS providers, hospital networks, and public agencies. Its broader goal is to establish a U.S. hub for emergency innovation, integrating AI, logistics, and medical readiness to deliver faster, smarter, and more effective response systems nationwide.
###  SPP167 | Food & Beverage
United Kingdom
Food & Beverage
**SIC:** 7373
**NAICS:** 541519
###  SPP170 | Construction
France
Construction
**SIC:** 8713
**NAICS:** 541360
**Project Description:** Established in 2009, this French company specializes in underground network detection and mapping particularly in the construction industry. Utilizing their modeling and detection technologies as well as their training platform, the company works with clients to secure construction sites and feed geospatial databases for local authorities and operators. In France, the company operates through a franchise model working closely with 25 agencies across the country. They are interested in exploring a co-licensing agreement to roll out their detection and mapping technologies in the United States with the goal of establishing a franchise in Pennsylvania. The company is interested in exploring partnership with public works companies, technical design offices, companies specialized in topography or geophysics, service providers for local municipalities, or local contractors seeking diversification through a high value-added technical franchise.
###  SPP172 | EdTech
France
EdTech
**SIC:** 7371
**NAICS:** 541511
**Project Description:** A French IT company specializing in education, accessibility, and assistive technologies has adapted several assistive reading tools that makes text more accessible through real-time visual and structural adaptations. Designed for both students and educators, the tool enhances reading comfort, confidence, and learning outcomes. The technology adapts to each student’s specific needs, provides personalized learning experiences that improve reading, comprehension, and overall learning outcome. The company is hoping to pilot and scale this innovative tool in the United States to address the challenges educators face in supporting and helping diagnosed students with dyslexia. The company is looking for a strategic partner with strong connections to school districts, state education departments, or universities.
The ideal partner will have strong history of working with educational institutions in the United States and experience working with legislative bodies, state and federal agencies, and advocacy groups. The ideal Pennsylvania-based partner should also have the capabilities and network to integrate the new platform into existing marketing and sales strategies.

Why Pennsylvania?
#  Strategic Location with **Global Access**
![Philadelphia under a hazy purple sunset. An incoming train crosses Ben Franklin Bridge](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/philadelphia-shutterstock_251305933?fmt=webp)
## A Clear Path to Market
Located at the heart of the Northeast and Mid-Atlantic regions, the Keystone State offers unmatched access to major American markets. Whether you're scaling up or starting fresh, Pennsylvania's intermodal infrastructure is key to success. Located within a day’s drive of nearly 40% of the U.S. population and 60% of Canadians, Pennsylvania positions companies for success. Our robust infrastructure, backed by 5,600 miles of rail and 120,000 miles of state and local highways, keeps businesses connected and competitive.
A powerhouse for global trade, Pennsylvania's ports handle over 67 million tons of goods annually. From the Atlantic Ocean via [Philadelphia(opens in a new tab)](https://www.philaport.com/ "Link to Port website") to the Gulf of Mexico through [Pittsburgh(opens in a new tab)](https://www.portpitt.com/) or the Great Lakes from [Erie(opens in a new tab)](https://www.porterie.org/), our ports ensure seamless access to national and international markets. Add to that six international airports and over 125 regional airports, which move more than 600,000 tons of materials and 35 million passengers annually. Whether shipping goods or attracting talent, Pennsylvania is the keystone in business strategy. Here, you can count on flexible transportation options to stay competitive in a fast-paced market and conveniently move goods to any destination.
The state's diverse energy resources ensure reliable, cost-efficient power for operations and logistics. As one of the top producers of natural gas and electricity in the U.S., the Commonwealth delivers energy affordability and stability across industries. And we're investing in renewable energy to fuel sustainable growth for the future.
Because in Pennsylvania, it's not just about getting there — it's about getting it done.
![A map showing Pennsylvania relative to other East Coast states and Canada, with the placement of major cities noted.](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/dced/2024-proximity-map-pagetsitdone-website.jpg)
## Learn about our Foreign Trade Zones
With eight Foreign Trade Zones (FTZs) in the state, foreign companies have ample opportunity to take advantage of the various benefits of locating within a FTZ in Pennsylvania.
[ EXPLORE FOREIGN TRADE ZONES (opens in a new tab)](https://ofis.trade.gov/Zones)
![A Wan Hei Lines cargo ship, loaded up with shipping containers, docked at the Port of Philadelphia on a sunny day. Large port cargo cranes are visible in the background.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/22282_gov_philaport_dz_038tioga%20marine%20terminal_portphila)
The success of Pennsylvania’s ports is no accident. Building on its central placement between the Northeast and the Mid-Atlantic, the state has heavily invested in building out ports and sea networks to open up commerce and trade. Our three major ports — [Port of Philadelphia(opens in a new tab)](https://www.philaport.com/ "Link to Port of Philadelphia website"), [Port of Pittsburgh(opens in a new tab)](https://www.portpitt.com/ "Link to Port of Pittsburgh website"), and [Port of Erie(opens in a new tab)](https://www.porterie.org/ "Link to Port of Erie website") — each contribute unique advantages for in-state and global companies. Over 67 million tons of goods come through our ports each year, representing nearly $50 billion in value, and the Port of Philadelphia in particular is consistently ranked [the top performing port(opens in a new tab)](https://www.ajot.com/news/philadelphia-ranks-1-in-north-america-for-productivity-for-the-second-year-in-a-row) in the country.
![Freight trains at the Pennsylvania railway museum](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/railroad_museum_pennsylvania_craig_benner_2010)
Pennsylvania leads the U.S. with 65 operating railroads and more than
Our more than[in 2024 alone,(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/penndot/interactive-pages/results/results.html#:~:text=2024%20In%20Review%20488%20bridges%20were%20let,2024.%20This%20includes%202%2C186%20miles%20of%20paving. "Link to Commonwealth infrastructure website") the Pennsylvania Department of Transportation and partners improved or replaced 488 bridges and 5,910 miles of roadway.
![Freight trains at the Pennsylvania railway museum](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/railroad_museum_pennsylvania_craig_benner_2010)
![Engine of white commercial airplane docked on apron outside airport terminal. Unrecognisable worker under the wing. Sunny day. Ground service theme.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/adobestock_435903113)
Going global in Pennsylvania is hassle-free thanks to six international airports, providing fast connections to major markets. The [Philadelphia International Airport(opens in a new tab)](https://www.phl.org/ "Link to Philadelphia International Airport website"), [Pittsburgh International Airport(opens in a new tab)](https://flypittsburgh.com/ "Link to Pittsburgh International Airport Website"), [Wilkes-Barre/Scranton International Airport(opens in a new tab)](https://flyavp.com/ "Link to Wilkes-Barre/Scranton International Airport Website"), [Harrisburg International Airport(opens in a new tab)](https://www.flyhia.com/ "Link to Harrisburg International Airport Website"), [Lehigh-Northampton Airport(opens in a new tab)](https://www.flyabe.com/ "Link to Northampton International Airport Website"), and the [Erie International Airport (opens in a new tab)](https://www.erieairport.org/ "Link to Erie International Airport Website")all offer nonstop domestic and international flights, and our 125 regional airports make local and private travel a breeze.
Our airports are growing, too; not only are carriers continuously adding additional routes and flights, but a [new terminal(opens in a new tab)](https://flypittsburgh.com/acaa-corporate/new-terminal-overview/) at Pittsburgh International Airport and [ongoing improvements(opens in a new tab)](https://www.constructionequipmentguide.com/upgraded-philadelphia-international-airport-readies-for-visitors-in-2026/69635) at Philadelphia International Airport will help welcome new travelers in 2026 and beyond.

# International **Trade**
![Cargo cranes on a dock at the Port of Philadelphia on a cloudy day](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/20514_gov_ports_dz_002?fmt=webp)
## Export Assistance for **Pennsylvania Companies**
Pennsylvania products and services travel to 213 markets worldwide and represent 5.5% percent of Pennsylvania’s GDP. Exporting from PA is the smart way to expand your company's reach to new markets while reaping the benefits of the Commonwealth's competitive business environment. That's why we offer one of the largest, most comprehensive state-sponsored international trade programs in the United States. Whether you have questions about foreign regulations, are seeking a qualified business partner in a new market, or need general assistance, we're here to help, contact our international trade team to get started.
## **How We Can Help**
BusinessPA's international trade team, along with our partners, offer confidential and customized programs and services to help Pennsylvania-based companies grow their international sales. With headquarters in Harrisburg, local support in 10 regional offices across the state through our [Regional Export Network (REN)](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/trade/regional_export_network "Link to Regional Export Network website") partners, and [13 PA Authorized Trade Representatives (ATRs)](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/trade/authorized-trade-representatives "Link to 13 PA Authorized Trade Representatives website") around the world, we are here to help your company reach new markets.
## Our Services
  * Guide ​you through export processes & market entry strategy development.​
    * Market Overview​
    * Market Entry Strategy​
    * Certifications / Standards / Regulatory Requirements​
    * Patent / Copyright / Trademark Information​
    * Education programs and technical support


  * Coordinate your business trips with our on-the-ground, in-country teams.
    * Appointment Setting​
    * Trip / Travel Logistics


  * Support you on international trade missions and at international trade shows.
    * Trade Event Support​
    * Marketing & Promotional Literature Review


  * Access to grant and financing programs.


![An puzzle piece-styled infographic. It reads: "DCED BusinessPA. Looking for a qualified partner? Wrestling with foreign regulations? Handling a trade lead from another country and need guidance? 10 Regional Export Network Partners. 13 Authorized Trade Representatives.](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/trade/Puzzle%20Piece%20Updated.png)
![David Briel headshot](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/David%20Briel)

![A group of businesspeople pose for a picture in front of a window](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/BTW2PA%20ATR%20Group%20Photo%20Central%20PA)
## Bringing the World to PA
Every year, the BusinessPA team hosts **Bringing the World to PA** to connect Pennsylvania businesses and educational institutions with global opportunities through our network of Authorized Trade Representatives. 
In 2025, the Bringing the World to PA tour hosted ten events across the Commonwealth and supported growing businesses across a wide range of industries. Stay tuned for information about future events in 2026!
[ LEARN ABOUT THE EVENT](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/trade/bringing_the_world_to_pa)
![A group of businesspeople pose for a picture in front of a window](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/BTW2PA%20ATR%20Group%20Photo%20Central%20PA)
## Resources
### Global Access Program (GAP)
The Global Access Program (GAP) is designed to enhance the capability of small to mid-sized Pennsylvania companies to increase export sales. GAP is administered by BusinessPA and provides up to $10,000 per award period to qualifying Pennsylvania companies to reimburse up to 75% of eligible expenses associated with specific export promotion activities. The program is funded in part through a federal grant with the U.S. Small Business Administration.
[LEARN MORE ABOUT GAP(opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/global-access-program-gap)
### US Department of Commerce 
New to exporting? The International Trade Administration offers online resources that outline the important steps companies should take to become a successful exporter.
[Learn about the Department of Commerce(opens in a new tab)](https://www.trade.gov/learn-how-export)

International Trade
# Regional **Export** Network
![A group of Regional Export Network officials, in business attire, pose for a group photo in a conference room](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1722954449354?fmt=webp)
## Lean on Our In-State Network of Trade Experts
Staffed by professional business development consultants, the **Regional Export Network (REN)** serves as the first point of contact for our clients. REN partners provide export development services to manufacturers and service firms located within their territory.
## Services include:
  * Export counseling
  * Market research and market entry strategy development
  * Education programs and technical support


Use arrow keys to choose tabs. Content for the chosen tab will be revealed below.

International Trade
#  Trade **Success Stories**
![A mobile crane lifts a shipping container onto a stack of colorful shipping containers at a port](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/PhilaPort%20Shipping%20Containers%20and%20Crane?fmt=webp)
## Helping Companies Reach **New Markets**
Through our International Trade program, every year we provide hands-on support to hundreds of Pennsylvania companies looking to do business across the globe. By leveraging our network of global trade partners, providing access to resources and information, and helping companies make critical business connections, we're invested in your international plans. Take a look at what we accomplished recently, and check out a few stories from companies we've helped get stuff done.
* * *
[ ![Daisy Data company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/trade/trade-success-stories/logos/daisy%20data.png) ](https://www.daisydata.com/)
[ ![ITSI Biosciences Logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/trade/trade-success-stories/logos/itsi-biosciences-logo%20\(1\).png) ](https://itsibio.com/?srsltid=AfmBOopdqutF5-E-bWWRWc28vJ9qOTiD7M2Jcl1ovFMMXSODzAJkEO_g)
[ ![Lampire Biological company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/trade/trade-success-stories/logos/lbl-logo%20w-dot.png) ](https://www.lampire.com/)
[ ![Megator company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/trade/trade-success-stories/logos/megator-new-2020-logo-aug6.png) ](https://www.megator.com/)
[ ![Parcel Health company logo](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/image/general-page-imagery/trade/trade-success-stories/logos/parcel%20health%20navy+logo.png) ](https://www.parcelhealth.co/)

##  $534.3 Million Export sales reported by companies who received BusinessPA assistance 
## Pennsylvania Companies are Exporting Globally.

![A man wearing a suit smiles for a picture in a brightly lit office lobby with many windows and modern furniture](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1%20-%20itsibio%20-%20dr%20richard%20somiari%20-%20picture)
## **ITSI Biosciences’ Market Development Efforts in Africa Pay Off, Awarded Contract in Nigeria**
Based out of Johnstown, PA, ITSI Biosciences worked with the BusinessPA team to get their products exported to Nigeria. Read their story and discover how our team can help connect you with opportunities around the world.
[ READ ITSI BIO CASE STUDY](https://pagetsitdone.com/locate_or_expand/trade/trade_success_stories/success_story_itsibio)
![A man wearing a suit smiles for a picture in a brightly lit office lobby with many windows and modern furniture](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1%20-%20itsibio%20-%20dr%20richard%20somiari%20-%20picture)

## **Parcel Health Disrupting Pharma Packaging, Makes First Sale to Canada**
Discover how this women-led PA manufacturing company worked with BusinessPA to get their products—safe, sustainable containers for pills—introduced to the Canadian market.

Why Pennsylvania?
# Pennsylvania Works **Smarter**
![Governor Josh Shapiro with Amazon Employees holding the ribbon during inauguration](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/23952_gov_amazon_dz_016-copy-1?fmt=webp)
##  The Fuel for **Future-Forward Thinking**
### **So, why PA?** Maybe a better question is: why go anywhere else?
Pennsylvania delivers an experienced workforce, world class higher education institutions, and a prime East Coast location near four of the nation’s 10 largest markets. All that, plus an exceptional quality of life. Here, innovation thrives with vibrant communities and a dynamic business ecosystem dedicated to getting it done.
Home to the innovative and ingenious, Pennsylvania is the most economically diverse state in the nation. We’re a powerful energy producer, leader in academic research, and hub of agriculture and advanced manufacturing. And we’re ready to fuel business success. Our business-friendly tax climate is designed for growth — we’re on track to cut the corporate net income tax rate down to 4.99% by 2031, making it among the lowest in the nation. Combine that with nationally ranked universities fostering top talent and a robust transportation infrastructure that connects companies to the world, and you’ll see why Pennsylvania is a place where big ideas grow — and so can businesses. Home to 20 Fortune 500 companies, state-of-the-art R&D facilities, and more than one million small businesses, Pennsylvania is where a rich history meets your promising future.
## Navigation Cards
### [Location & Infrastructure ](https://pagetsitdone.com/why-pa/location_and_infrastructure)

### A prime East Coast location with
### an **exceptional** quality of life

#1 Best Business School (University of Pennsylvania, Wharton) [ U.S. News & World Report, 2025 (opens in a new tab)](https://www.usnews.com/best-graduate-schools/top-business-schools/mba-rankings)
20 Number of Fortune 500 Companies Located in Pennsylvania  [ Visual Capitalist, 2024 (opens in a new tab)](https://www.visualcapitalist.com/map-the-number-of-fortune-500-companies-in-each-u-s-state/)

26th Largest Economy in the World [ World Bank Group, 2024 (opens in a new tab)](https://datacatalog.worldbank.org/search/dataset/0038130)

Newsletter
#  Stay In the Know with PA's Latest**Business Wins**
![A rendering of the PA Gets it Done newsletter](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/newsletter3dv2?fmt=webp)
We get it – business moves quickly in Pennsylvania. That’s why we’ve created the BusinessPA newsletter, a convenient way to stay up-to-date with all things economic development in the Commonwealth. Every month, we’ll share important news, business resources, funding opportunities, investment wins, and so much more, highlighting why Pennsylvania is the best place for business.
As a bonus for signing up, you’ll receive information about Pennsylvania’s powerful tax advantages — and some of them may surprise you!

Why Pennsylvania?
# A Business Climate **Built for Action**
![Governor Josh Shapiro, surrounded by a group of government officials and business leaders, smiles and shows an exectutive order document for the just-announced Permit Fast Track program. The Philadelphia skyline and construction equipment are visible in the distance.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/1732114707765?fmt=webp)
## Boosting business success through **collaborative, smart policy.**
Pennsylvania’s diverse regions and vibrant economy — ranked the 26th largest in the world — make it a launchpad for businesses across sectors. From robotics and life sciences research centers to thriving hubs of manufacturing and agriculture, Pennsylvania offers prime locations across the state for your business to grow and succeed​​. We're proud to be the [only Northeastern state with a growing economy](https://pagetsitdone.com/news/new-report--pennsylvania-the-only-northeastern-state-with-a-grow), and our targeted support for growing companies is why we're one of the [top-ranked business climates](https://pagetsitdone.com/news/new-report--pa-named-one-of-the-top-business-climates-in-the-nat) in the country.
We’re not just good for business, we’re ready for action. Pennsylvania has a clear 10-year [economic development strategy](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/copa-getsitdone/en/documents/economicdevelopmentstrategy-dced_2024_final.pdf), with significant investments in infrastructure, workforce training, and site development. Through programs like [PA SITES](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/pennsylvania-strategic-investments-to-enhance-sites-program-pa-sites/), we are fast-tracking projects to make more industrial and commercial sites shovel-ready — so your business can hit the ground running.
## Lower rates and fewer barriers **give companies an edge.**
Here in Pennsylvania, we’re taking bold steps to boost our tax competitiveness. Cutting the corporate net income tax rate to 4.99% by 2031 is just the tip of the iceberg. Learn why the Keystone State is among the most attractive states to do business
  * **Reduced Corporate Net Income Tax (CNIT) Rate**
    * Decreasing 0.5% annually from 7.49% in 2026 to 4.99% in 2031, Pennsylvania’s corporate net income tax rate is becoming one of the most competitive regionally and nationally. Once fully phased down, the rate will be lower than all of our neighboring states that have CNITs, where rates currently range from 6.5% (West Virginia) all the way up to 11.5% (New Jersey).


  * **Personal Income Tax (PIT) Rate: 3.07%**
    * With a flat 3.07% tax that applies to partnerships, LLCs, and S corporations, Pennsylvania is prime for small and medium-sized businesses that operate as pass-through entities. Of states with a PIT, only two states — Arizona (2.5%) and North Dakota (2.9%) — have lower rates.


  * **Tangible Personal Property Tax: 0%**
    * Pennsylvania does not tax machinery, equipment, or inventories — a tax imposed in 27 other states. This removes barriers to capital investment and makes business expansion more cost-effective.


  * **Increasing Allowable NOL Deductions**
    * The state is increasing allowable Net Operating Loss (NOL) deductions by 10% annually — from 40% in 2025 up to the federal limit of 80% in 2029. This change supports innovation in start-up, technology, and life sciences businesses.


  * **Broad Sales and Use Tax Exemptions for Manufacturing and R &D**
    * Pennsylvania offers broad exemptions for manufacturing and R&D-related purchases, reducing acquisition costs and supporting business upgrades.


  * **Faster Permitting, Fewer Roadblocks**
    * The [PA Permit Fast Track Program](https://www.pa.gov/agencies/oto/fasttrack) and the Department of Envrionmental Protection's [SPEED Program](https://www.pa.gov/services/dep/speed) provide tailored assistance to help expedite permitting deciscions, so you can get from groundbreaking to grand opening faster.


> Everyone at BusinessPA... did whatever they could to help connect us and make things move quicker."
-  _Ted McKlveen, Co-founder & CEO, [Verne](https://pagetsitdone.com/key_industries/energy/case-study-verne)_

Why Pennsylvania?
# Embrace a World-Class **Quality of Life**
![An outdoor cafe patio in a historic Pennsylvania town on a cloudy day](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Warren-MainStreet-1?fmt=webp)
## In Pennsylvania, we don't just work hard — we live life to the fullest.
Whether you’re seeking an urban cultural center or a quieter rural life, a lifestyle that fits you awaits in PA — a state that wholeheartedly embraces the importance of work-life balance.
We do more than just work hard — we live fully. Ranked among the top ten states for [quality of life(opens in a new tab)](https://wallethub.com/edu/best-states-to-live-in/62617 "Link to Wallethub article")​, PA provides a perfect blend of affordability and access to culture and recreation. From vibrant cities like Philadelphia and Pittsburgh to charming suburbs and small towns regularly recognized on [best-of lists(opens in a new tab)](https://www.niche.com/places-to-live/search/best-places-to-live/s/pennsylvania/ "Link to Niche.com article"), this is a place where both your employees and your family can thrive.
We’re proud to be home to world-class education and healthcare systems, including [two of the top children’s hospitals in the country(opens in a new tab)](https://health.usnews.com/health-news/best-childrens-hospitals/articles/best-childrens-hospitals-honor-roll-and-overview "Link to US News health article")​. Pennsylvania’s commitment to education shines brightly throughout the state with its [high-performing school districts(opens in a new tab)](https://www.niche.com/k12/search/best-school-districts/s/pennsylvania/ "Link to Niche.com school districts article") and [seven of the top 100 universities(opens in a new tab)](https://www.usnews.com/best-colleges/pa?_sort=rank&_sortDirection=asc) in the U.S.
Close to both the Midwest and the East Coast, the Keystone State's prime location — paired with our [reputation for stunning outdoor scenery(opens in a new tab)](https://10best.usatoday.com/awards/best-destination-for-fall-colors/ "Link to USA Today article") — make it a great state to grow your business while enjoying a high quality of life. World-class hiking, camping, skiing and countless other outdoor activities are only a short drive away from our bustling cities and cozy small towns, so you can enjoy all the benefits that Pennsylvania has to offer no matter where you want to live,
Pennsylvania has also earned a reputation as a housing haven, where affordability reigns supreme. Whether you prefer to live in [bustling urban centers like Pittsburgh(opens in a new tab)](https://www.realtor.com/news/trends/pittsburgh-pennsylvania-most-affordable-large-housing-market/), or growing cities like Harrisburg and Lancaster, PA boasts a low cost of living compared to many northeastern states. In fact, we're one of the [most affordable northeastern states for first-time homebuyers(opens in a new tab)](https://www.realtor.com/advice/hyperlocal/salary-you-need-to-buy-home-pennsylvania/), putting homeownership in reach for more people and making it easier to enjoy a high quality of life here, no matter what you do.
> The collaborative nature of businesses, economic, educational, and philanthropic organizations in the area that continually work to improve the quality of life here make it an outstanding location for our company, our employees, and their families."
_— Seifi Ghasemi, CEO of Air Products (Lehigh Valley)_
Use arrow keys to choose tabs. Content for the chosen tab will be revealed below. 
Top-Ranked Quality of Life  Exceptional Education  Arts, Cuisine, and Culture  Great Outdoors 
  * Top-Ranked Quality of Life
  * Exceptional Education
  * Arts, Cuisine, and Culture
  * Great Outdoors


![An aerial image of Bedford, PA. Buildings, roads and foliage extend into the distance, surrounded by forest-covered mountains and a blue sky.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/25986_gov_keystonecomm_erd_004)
WalletHub ranks Pennsylvania among the [top ten states for quality of life(opens in a new tab)](https://wallethub.com/edu/best-states-to-live-in/62617 "Link to Wallethub Quality of Life ranking"), and CNBC puts us in the [top 10 for affordability(opens in a new tab)](https://www.cnbc.com/2024/07/12/americas-10-cheapest-states-to-live-in.html) — the only state on the East Coast to make the list. Suburbs like Chesterbrook earn accolades as the [best places to raise a family(opens in a new tab)](https://www.niche.com/places-to-live/search/best-places-for-families/ "Link to Niche Best Places for Family article"), with four Pennsylvania communities being among the best in the country. And for first-time homebuyers, we're one of the [most affordable(opens in a new tab)](https://www.realtor.com/advice/hyperlocal/salary-you-need-to-buy-home-pennsylvania/) Northeastern states to buy a home.
![An aerial image of Bedford, PA. Buildings, roads and foliage extend into the distance, surrounded by forest-covered mountains and a blue sky.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/25986_gov_keystonecomm_erd_004)
![](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Penn_State_adobestock_533167539)
On top of our continued investments in our K-12 schools, Pennsylvania's ecosystem of nearly 300 postsecondary institutions has something for everyone. We're home to three of the nation's [top 50 universities(opens in a new tab)](https://www.usnews.com/best-colleges/pa?_sort=rank&_sortDirection=asc "US News rankings for top universities"), but innovation is happening everywhere - from the thriving robotics and engineering scene in Pittsburgh, to the cutting-edge life sciences research happening in Lehigh Valley.
Pennsylvania colleges are recognized for their track record of [producing future leaders(opens in a new tab)](https://time.com/7333710/best-colleges-future-leaders-2026/), giving companies a robust talent pipeline to help them grow. We're also continuously investing in workforce development programs, helping support careers in our in-demand industires - from manufacturing to agriculture, and beyond.
![](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Penn_State_adobestock_533167539)
![A crowd explore a colorful arts and culure festival on a closed-off street in downtown Lebanon, PA.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/lebo%20unveiled)
Whatever your interests are, you'll never run out things to experience in Pennsylvania. For art aficionados, PA is home to over 80 art museums, including the iconic [Philadelphia Museum of Art(opens in a new tab)](https://www.philamuseum.org/ "Link to Philadelphia Museum of Art website") and the [Andy Warhol Museum(opens in a new tab)](https://www.warhol.org/ "Andy Warhol Museum official website"). We're also home to world-class music venues hosting local talent like the [Philadelphia Orchestra(opens in a new tab)](https://philorch.ensembleartsphilly.org/ "The Philadelphia Orchestra official website"), and big-name bands regularly make tour stops at venues like [Hersheypark Stadium(opens in a new tab)](https://www.hersheyentertainment.com/hersheypark-stadium/ "Link to Hersheypark Stadium official website").
For foodies hungry for something new, check out Pennsylvania's [Michelin-star restaurants(opens in a new tab)](https://www.abc27.com/pennsylvania/pennsylvania-earns-first-michelin-star-restaurants/), serving up unforgettable dining experiences. We also boast [over 530 craft breweries(opens in a new tab)](https://www.brewersassociation.org/statistics-and-data/state-craft-beer-stats/?state=PA), ranking third in the nation, and [more than 400 wineries(opens in a new tab)](https://pennsylvaniawine.com/about "Link to Pennsylvania WIneries official website"). Whatever your drink of choice, cheers to that.
![A crowd explore a colorful arts and culure festival on a closed-off street in downtown Lebanon, PA.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/lebo%20unveiled)
![A riverside town nestled among the mountains during autumn.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/tidioute-warrencovisitorsbureau)
From water trails and hiking, to snowsports and biking, Pennsylvania is full of opportunities to get the blood pumping and to soak in Vitamin D. With 86,000 miles of streams and rivers, over 6,700 miles of hiking trails, 125 free state parks, and 20 ski resorts, there are outdoor opportunities for everyone. Thrill seekers can take on hiking paths on the [Appalachian Trail(opens in a new tab)](https://appalachiantrail.org/explore/explore-by-state/pennsylvania/ "Link to Applachian Trail official website") or take a lift up to [Blue Knob Ski Resort(opens in a new tab)](https://blueknob.com/ "Link to official website fro Blue Knob") for the most challenging slopes in the state, while relaxation enthusiasts can enjoy beaches at [Presque Isle State Park(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/agencies/dcnr/recreation/where-to-go/state-parks/find-a-park/presque-isle-state-park.html "Link to Presque Isle State Park website") or birdwatch at the famous [Hawk Mountain(opens in a new tab)](https://www.hawkmountain.org/ "Link to Hawk Mountain official website").
Our four seasons bring the fun year-round — whether it’s leaf-peeping in the fall, skiing in the winter, or kayaking in the summer. Whether you want adventure or escape, PA has no shortage of ways to get some fresh air away from it all.
![A riverside town nestled among the mountains during autumn.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/tidioute-warrencovisitorsbureau)
#1 Best Large City for Home Buying (Pittsburgh)  [ Realtor.com, 2025 (opens in a new tab)](https://www.realtor.com/news/trends/pittsburgh-pennsylvania-most-affordable-large-housing-market/)
#1 Best Small Town for Arts and Culture (New Hope)  [ Travel + Leisure, 2024 (opens in a new tab)](https://www.travelandleisure.com/americas-best-small-towns-of-2024-8699455#toc-best-small-arts--culture-town)
#10 Top State to Live In [ Wallethub, 2025 (opens in a new tab)](https://wallethub.com/edu/best-states-to-live-in/62617)

Why Pennsylvania?
#  Workforce and **Education**
![Ben Franklin Technology Development Authority BFTDA - via Innovation Works -PECA Labs was founded by a group of Carnegie Mellon alumni including a pediatric surgeon, PECA Labs is revolutionizing cardiovascular implantable devices with a polymer platform and a novel design approach. PECA Labs is a medical device development company focused on bringing new solutions to underserved populations: Our first product, the Masa Valve, is a surgeon-created, engineer-optimized, clinically-implanted and validated heart valve.](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/pecalabs_16590116834_0d11930074_o?fmt=webp)
## Developing **Next-Level** Talent
Your ability to adapt to changes and meet opportunity head-on is dependent on the quality of your team, and Pennsylvania is ready to power your business with a workforce of nearly 6.5 million strong. Our talent pool isn’t just large — it’s diverse, dynamic, and prepared to meet changing demands across every industry. Whether it’s advanced manufacturing, life sciences research, or education, we’re investing in a labor force that’s well-trained for innovation. 
With nearly 300 higher-ed and post-secondary institutions fueling our talent pipeline — including top-ranked powerhouses like the [University of Pennsylvania(opens in a new tab)](https://www.upenn.edu/) and [Carnegie Mellon University(opens in a new tab)](https://www.cmu.edu/) — PA doesn’t just educate, we empower. Our extensive apprenticeship programs and workforce training grants go beyond traditional learning, equipping workers with future-focused skills in high-demand fields from agriculture to energy. Whether you’re looking for team members capable of supporting manufacturing operations, spearheading R&D and innovation, handling logistics and supply chain needs, or running your corporate headquarters, Pennsylvanians can get the job done.
The Keystone State is invested in bringing businesses and qualified workers together. We’ll help you find or develop your workforce, from apprentices to experienced experts and everyone in between. If you’re looking to upskill your employees or connect with leaders in your industry, we can help with our customizable and flexible workforce programs.
> “We are grateful for our partnership with Pennsylvania’s Department of Community and Economic Development. The Training-to-Career grant funding supports our collective efforts to prepare the next generation of skilled workers for good-paying jobs in high demand fields.” 
_— Patrick M. Jones, President and CEO, Bucks County Community College_
![Gwen Ross smiling, with a building behind her](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/gwenaross_headshot)
## Gwen A. Ross
Director of Workforce Development Initiatives
gwross@pa.gov | 717.720.7386

### Explore the Data: Pennsylvania's Workforce
_Data Disclaimer: The data on this page is updated twice a year, so may not be the latest available. Looking for the most current Pennsylvania data and statistics? We can help. ContactDebbie Tollett in the Strategic Information Services Office to get started with your inquiry._
## Workforce Development Guide
Investing in training and retaining top talent is a priority for Pennsylvania. We have specialized technical and financial assistance to help your business develop the right workforce.
[ DOWNLOAD THE GUIDE (opens in a new tab)](https://pagetsitdone.com/content/dam/dced/documents/new/workforcedev-brochure_2023v2.pdf)
![Old Main at Penn State University](https://s7d9.scene7.com/is/image/statepa/Penn_State_adobestock_533167539)
## Education
In PA, we pride ourselves on our ability to turn out creative thinkers, inventors, and game changers – and the world has taken notice. Our culture is one that encourages innovation and collaboration. That's why domestic and international businesses alike cite our world-class higher education and research institutions, including the [Wharton School of Business(opens in a new tab)](https://www.wharton.upenn.edu/ "Link to Wharton School of Business website") and [Penn Law(opens in a new tab)](https://www.law.upenn.edu/ "Link to Penn Law website"), [Penn State University(opens in a new tab)](https://www.psu.edu/), [Lehigh University(opens in a new tab)](https://www1.lehigh.edu/ "Link to Lehigh University website"), [Carnegie Mellon University(opens in a new tab)](https://www.cmu.edu/ "Link to Carnegie Mellon University website"), and [University of Pittsburgh(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pitt.edu/ "Link to University of Pittsburgh website") as a key driver of developing talent and inspiring big ideas at their companies.
But it's not just the big-name schools fueling our workforce pipelines. Our [15 community colleges(opens in a new tab)](https://www.education.pa.gov/Postsecondary-Adult/CollegeCareer/Pages/Community-Colleges.aspx "Link to PA Department of Education website") offer a wide range of 2-year and certificate programs that meet the needs of local industry and community. And [Pennsylvania's 14 four-year public universities(opens in a new tab)](https://www.passhe.edu/universities/index.html#:~:text=Cheyney%20University,West%20Chester%20University "Link to website with information PA universities") are a critical resource for both residents and employers. These institutions play an important role in helping local businesses stay nimble and up to date with the latest technology and provide training for their current and future workers.
Home to[ the #1 business school(opens in a new tab)](https://www.usnews.com/best-graduate-schools/top-business-schools/mba-rankings "Link to US News article on business schoosl") in the country, [a top 10 law school(opens in a new tab)](https://www.usnews.com/best-graduate-schools/top-law-schools/law-rankings "Link to US News article on law schools"), and seven[ universities ranked in the top 100 nationwide(opens in a new tab)](https://www.usnews.com/best-colleges/pa "Link to US News article on university rankings"), it is no surprise that Pennsylvania grads are highly sought-after for their competitive edge and drive. Our world-renowned institutions ensure that PA's workforce pipeline is filled with critical thinkers, problem-solvers, innovators, and dreamers. And our vibrant and dynamic communities, coupled with a long list of top employers in the state, ensures that those highly sought-after graduates stay in the Keystone State.
* * *
### Discover our colleges, universities, and trade schools
[ EXPLORE SCHOOLS (opens in a new tab)](https://nces.ed.gov/collegenavigator/?s=PA)

### Explore our interactive talent report
[ View Report (opens in a new tab)](https://properties.zoomprospector.com/PA/ic?token=pSrOQr_iI&id=r264&objectType=community&reportName=talent&talentDefaultToSchools=true&talentDefaultToCommunity=true&isMicroScript=&radius=)
###  Industrial Resource Centers (IRCs)
Part of the statewide Manufacturing PA Initiative, the IRCs are a network of regional organizations focused on assisting manufacturers with growth strategies and staying competitive in a changing global economy. Workforce development consultations are part of their many available services. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.pamade.org/)
###  Pennsylvania’s Industry Partnerships
Pennsylvania’s Industry Partnerships (IPs) are regional industrial partnerships of businesses in a shared labor market who work with multiple teams to address overall competitiveness of the industry. Employers are welcome to join their local IPs for networking, collaboration, and setting sustainable initiatives. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.dli.pa.gov/Businesses/Workforce-Development/Pages/Industry-Partnerships.aspx)
###  WEDnetPA Workforce Grants
The Workforce & Economic Development Network of Pennsylvania (WEDnetPA) is a DCED-funded workforce training program helping employers upskill employees to fill in employment gaps. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](http://www.wednetpa.com/)
###  Foundations in Industry Training (FIT) Grant
The DCED-funded Foundations in Industry Training (FIT) Grant Program can be used to help cover the costs of formal instruction or classroom requirements associated with apprenticeships. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/foundations-in-industry-training-fit-grant-program)
###  Manufacturing PA Training-to-Career Grant
The Manufacturing PA Training-to-Career Grant Program supports new and innovative training programs focused on developing the skill sets of entry-level applicants in the manufacturing industry to better meet the needs of hiring employers. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://dced.pa.gov/programs/manufacturing-pa-training-career-grant-program)
###  The Statewide Movement for Accountability, Readiness, & Training (PASmart)
The Statewide Movement for Accountability, Readiness, & Training (PASmart) is a multi-pronged workforce initiative supporting students, job seekers, and workers by connecting them with the information they need to succeed in our evolving economy. 
[ LEARN MORE (opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/agencies/education/programs-and-services/schools/grants-and-funding/school-grants/pasmart.html)
